Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
64
Compiled by the Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Path Desired by the Will
Is there anyone among the students present here who is seeing the teacher for the first time? If so, please raise your hand.
Teenagers pursuing the value of a new life
You all know that this high school period is the most precious time. Soon, some of you will finish your school years and enter society, while others may continue on the path of academia. It is the natural order of human life that after one era passes, another era arrives.
From the perspective of the will, the path of the will is not smooth. As you know, after the era of individual restoration passes, the era of family restoration comes, and after the era of family restoration, the era of national restoration follows, and after the era of national restoration, we advance to the era of world restoration. Since individuals, families, nations, and the world are different spheres, the environments and circumstances that unfold are also different.
As with everything, after you spend a day, a new morning comes the next day, but that morning is different from the morning of the previous day. Thus, as days pass, as months pass, as years pass, or as decades pass, the path of life inevitably progresses toward death.
October 22, 1972 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* This speech was given at the 17th Holy Spirit Conference (then high school 3rd year).
8   The Path Desired by the Will
When you reflect on your childhood, you may think it feels like a distant past, but especially the period from your teens to your twenties is the longest and most tedious time. When will I become twenty? When will I graduate from high school and go to university?
When will I be able to have the dignified spirit of a young adult and explore the true nature of life? This period from your teens to your twenties is indeed the most tedious time. By the time you reach the 4th or 5th grade of elementary school, you become a teenager, passing ten years old, graduating from that school, then entering middle school, and after that, entering high school and becoming a senior at twenty—though some may be over twenty—this period is the longest, and I believe you have felt it.
However, as you pass through your twenties and enter your thirties, the time from twenty to thirty feels increasingly shorter. The time from thirty to forty feels even quicker. The time from forty to fifty feels even closer. You will feel that as time goes on, it becomes shorter. In this view, the time when you most wish to grow older is between your teens and twenties.
So what happens as you grow older? You become an adult. What happens when you become an adult? You can discern everything. You can distinguish between good and evil, and you can find the worthwhile path of life by understanding that you should not go this way or that way. This is the time when you transition into your twenties. The tedium of the period from your teens to twenties is because there is an inner yearning to pursue the value of a new life, which makes it feel long.
During this time, some may have joined the Unification Church during middle school, while others may have joined during high school. There may be some who understood the will during elementary school or Sunday school, but the majority likely entered the path of the will during middle or high school. After knowing this path of the will, you must have discovered that your experience of your twenties before and after knowing the will is vastly different.
In the past, you may have thought you were pursuing the path of life you should take, filled with all your hopes, but after knowing the path of the will, your position has changed. You have come to feel that you must fulfill your responsibility to realize the will.
Soon, some of you will go to university, while others will enter society. In this situation, the most pressing question is, what is the path desired by the will?
You must understand that discerning what that path is and walking the correct path is very difficult.
Therefore, you must clearly understand what the path desired by the will, the true path desired by the will, is. Even at the moment when Jesus was concluding his fate on the cross, he said, “Abba, Father, not my will, but yours be done.” Even at the point of giving his life, he sought to walk the path desired by the will until the end. Moreover, for over thirty years, he struggled to align with the path desired by the will, experiencing rejection, hardship, and suffering in solitude, but all those circumstances and stories were solely for the purpose of establishing the path desired by the will.
Jesus himself struggled to walk the path desired by the will. His disciples, centered around Jesus, also set out to walk the path desired by the will. The group that looked to Jesus, who represented God, and sought to join the path of the will he desired were the apostles you know. Among them, the three chief disciples, Peter, James, and John, also set out to walk the path desired by the will. While Jesus walked the path desired by the will to the end, we know that Peter, James, John, and the other apostles experienced the historical sorrow of not fully walking the path desired by the will.
Despite having spent three years living, eating, and being with Jesus, there was a distance between the will Jesus envisioned and the will the disciples envisioned. There was also a distance between the nation Jesus envisioned and the nation the disciples envisioned. There was a distance between the world Jesus envisioned and the world the disciples envisioned. Depending on the perspective, we can infer that there were significant differences.
When viewed individually, Jesus was one individual, and someone like Peter was also one individual, but even when considering the individuals themselves, there was a distance. The individual known as Jesus represented history, was the central figure of the era, and was an individual who could boldly embark as the harbinger of future goodness, while the individual known as Peter was not an individual who could represent history, fulfill the mission of the era, or present a new beginning of goodness for the future. Such differences existed.
Because Jesus and the disciples stood in different positions, their paths were also different. Their standards of perception were different. Therefore, their feelings, purposes, and targets were also inevitably different. While Jesus sought to establish the will even at the point of giving his life, we know that the three disciples, Peter, James, and John, abandoned the will from a position of fearing death. 
Thus, although they were in the same environment at that time, eating together and acting together, the standards by which they viewed the will were different, resulting in a stark contrast in the outcomes of their lives, and we know that they bore those results.
The path that God desires is the path that the will desires.
From this perspective, although 180 students have gathered here, there must be one path. Among them are male and female students, but the path that students who truly seek the will must take is not two paths. Although there are differences in gender, the path for men and the path for women cannot be different. If a woman stands in front, the path a man must follow is that of the woman, and if a man stands in front, the path a woman must follow is that of the man. We must first understand that there can only be one path desired by the will.
In other words, the path taken by older people and the path taken by younger people cannot differ when it comes to the path desired by the will. In the process of fallen humanity ascending the path of restoration, there is not a multitude of paths. There is only one path, a straight line drawn as a single path. While there may be countless detours to the left and right of this straight path, there is only one path to walk straight ahead. If there is a true young person who sets out along that one path, it must be said that both men and women must walk the same path.
Then, what kind of path would be the most worthwhile and valuable path desired by the will? We can clearly understand through the teachings of Jesus and the teachings of the Bible that it is not a path taken for oneself. The true path of value desired by the will is not the path taken according to one’s own desires, but the path taken according to the will.
In other words, who is the subject of the will? It is God. It is the path taken according to God’s desires. In that path, there can be no personal wishes or personal intentions. Only after establishing God’s desires and God’s will can fallen humanity receive permission to inherit their own desires.
Since fallen humanity can only take their own wishes after fulfilling God’s desires, we must understand that we cannot have our own wishes or intentions.
Because Jesus came to this earth representing all humanity, he must serve as a standard in walking the path of the will and must embody a historical model in walking that path. Therefore, if Jesus walked through his youth, adulthood, and old age, then all humanity must follow the path he walked. Those in their youth must follow the path Jesus took in his youth, and those in adulthood must follow the path Jesus took in adulthood. Those in old age must follow the path Jesus took in his old age. You must understand that the path Jesus walked is a fateful path that everyone must take.
12   The Path Desired by the Will
Jesus and we are fundamentally different. Jesus came to this earth with the position of an unfallen son, but we humans have no qualifications to participate in the position of an unfallen son. Because we were born as fallen descendants, we must recognize that we stand in a position that cannot be compared to the unfallen son.
Therefore, in order for fallen beings to follow the Messiah, who is the unfallen son, they must possess various conditions to believe in him and follow him. Just following him does not mean you can simply do so without conditions. There must be a presentation of the content of indemnity, and by overcoming the conditions of that indemnity, there is a way to draw closer to the path of restoration.
What does the will require? It requires the position of unfallen Adam and Eve.
So how do we carry out the work of indemnity and restoration? We must walk the path in reverse to the position we fell from. Because of the fall, we must walk the opposite path of the unfallen way. What kind of path is that opposite path? It is a path that can be walked as unfallen beings.
Then, what is the position where unfallen beings can go and where God can dwell? It is the position where one can see unfallen Adam and Eve and where one can behold the archangel serving unfallen Adam and Eve.
What did humanity lose due to the fall? From the perspective centered on God’s will, the servant disappeared here. We lost the servant. What did we lose next? We lost sons and daughters. After losing sons and daughters, what did we lose? We lost the bride and groom. What did we lose next? We lost parents. In other words, we lost the servant, we lost sons and daughters, and we lost the bride and groom who could fulfill God’s ideal will through those sons and daughters. Thus, we lost everything.
Humanity fell, resulting in these outcomes, but what would have happened if we had not fallen? We would have had the archangel who faithfully served God until the end. We would have had true sons and daughters. God would have welcomed true bride and groom. Thus, through them, the relationship of true parents would have been realized in the position of unfallen beings. This is what God intended to achieve, which is God’s will. You must understand this.
When asked what God’s will is, you may answer, “It is the completion of the ideal of creation.” To fulfill the will means to complete the ideal of creation. What is the completion of the ideal of creation? It is the completion of the ideal of the four position foundation. What is the completion of the ideal of the four position foundation? It is to form true parents, true couples, and true children. Additionally, we must welcome true servants. This must be concluded as the standard of what God desires.
When asked what God’s will is, it may seem vague. When asked what God’s will is, it is to complete the ideal of creation. When the ideal of creation is completed, what happens? The ideal of the four position foundation is completed. When the ideal of the four position foundation is completed, what happens? It is to become one centered on God’s love. If that oneness is achieved, what would have happened? The archangels serving as servants would have gathered around them, who are the subject of love. This is God’s ideal of creation, that is, God’s will. Then, because of the fall, what are we seeking? We are seeking this. You must understand this.
As we ascend the path of restoration, what kind of content does God present to us and call us? First, we have become the descendants of servants. In other words, we have become the heirs of the archangel. What kind of being must an angel be? It must be one who serves God with complete loyalty and dedicates its whole life to God.
14   The Path Desired by the Will
It is something that must be honored. However, due to the fall, the pure laws and pure purposes of the servant could not be fulfilled. That is the result of the fall. 
In order for fallen humanity to return to the path of the will,
Therefore, fallen humans must engage in the history of the return of the servant. We must carry out the history of the return of the servant. 
Regarding humanity moving towards the future will of God, and the countless groups or created worlds that aspire to God's will, they must undergo training as servants who can honor the will and look towards it with hope. That is the play of religion.
That is why we are taught to serve people. Serve! Make sacrifices! This is the play that is taught. This is the foundational work in walking the path of God's will. In other words, to enter the path that God desires, we must first complete the connection of the relationship that has not fulfilled its mission as a servant. When we step forward to fulfill our responsibilities, we enter the path desired by God. We must understand this.
Then, what kind of groups exist on the path of restoration that God unfolds? There are those who can stand as true servants. While there are true servants, there are also those who can stand as wicked servants. After passing through that position, what kind of people are there? There is a position to stand as true sons and daughters. There must be a position to stand as true sons and daughters. After that, there is also a position to stand as false sons. This is represented in the Bible by Cain and Abel. The path of Abel is the true path, while the path of Cain is the false path. You must understand this. After passing through that path, there is a way to subdue Cain as Abel, achieving victory and completing the qualifications of bride and groom. This is the path of restoration today.
In other words, we have lost the servant, lost the sons and daughters, and lost the bride and groom, so we must seek the position to stand as bride and groom. The one who has completed Abel's mission will inherit the position to stand as the bridegroom, but only those born through the original love and lineage of God can stand in the position of the bridegroom. You must understand this.
Centered around the bride and groom, the origin where God's love can be harmonized is established on earth. This is achieved through the love of the bride and groom, and that position of the bride and groom is where the sons and daughters born with the direct love and bloodline of God mature and unite. However, today’s fallen humanity cannot simply participate in the position of sons and daughters who can stand as pure bride and groom because they were not born through God's love.
Therefore, we must complete the expectation for the Messiah by fulfilling the substantial expectation. How do we inherit the expectation for the Messiah? We must engage in the act of grafting ourselves to the Messiah. Through grafting, what was once a wild olive tree can be turned back into a true olive tree. In other words, by breaking free from the lineage of Satan and returning to the good lineage of God, we can only welcome the position of bride and groom from the position we are able to inherit.
What has religion sought out throughout historical times? It is to fulfill the mission as a servant. In the history of the wicked son and the good son, where they kill and take from each other, the path that has expanded the group capable of inheriting Abel's mission is the path that Christianity has walked until now.
However, it cannot directly ascend to the position of the son. Therefore, in order to inherit the position of the son and to connect this, the Messiah is needed. That person must be one who has come from the Father. He must have been born from the Father and grown up in the embrace of the Father’s love. This is where everything begins from the Father.
However, fallen humanity has not started from God the Father. We have started from the wicked Satan. Because we have started from wicked Satan, we must break free from it. We must break through it. We must achieve victory as individuals, as families, and on behalf of tribes, nations, and the world, raising the banner of rebellion and turning back to participate in the Abel-like position towards heaven; this is the path of restoration that you must understand.
To inherit the position of the son and advance to the position of bride and groom, what must we do? One has started to rise from the world of Satan, and one has started from God to connect and rise. The positions are different. You must understand that the failure to connect this is the tragedy of Christianity and the reason for the downfall of Judaism and the nation of Israel.
There is a way to change as a servant, and the wicked son can stand as a good son, but one cannot reach the complete position of a son that can inherit the true purpose of goodness. We must polish the good position and connect it to the true position of a son, advancing to the position of the bridegroom. Our lives must achieve oneness centered on God's love; otherwise, we cannot complete the expectation for the son-in-law. Therefore, the path of restoration and the path desired by the will is to reclaim that path.
The reason fallen humanity needs the Messiah
From God's perspective, there are true servants, true sons, and then there is the true bridegroom, through whom the true God emerges. On the side of Satan, there are false servants, false children, false bride and groom, and a false God. They are opposites. This must be cut off. We have fallen due to disobedience, disbelief, and disobedience to commands. Because we have fallen due to disbelief, disobedience, and disobedience, we must compensate for that in the opposite way.
Therefore, to become a true servant, one must have absolute faith, absolute obedience, and absolute submission. Without this, one cannot find the path that a true son or a good son walks. You must clearly understand this. You must fulfill your responsibilities as a servant, fulfill your responsibilities as a son, and then welcome the Messiah.
That is why Christianity also needs a Savior. The Lord must come again. After Jesus came during the time of Judaism, He must return again, which means the son must come again. This is an inevitable fact, but if that person does not appear, there is no way for me to find the original position I could have grown into as a child of God on this earth.
We were supposed to grow up and return to Satan's embrace, but in order to find the way back, we must come out from God and meet a representative who can connect us back. There is no other way than to be guided and transitioned. Therefore, what is absolutely necessary for fallen humanity is the Messiah. The Messiah is absolutely necessary. You must understand this. Why is the Messiah needed on the path of faith? If this issue is vague, you cannot go forward. "What do I need a Messiah for? Everyone is the same." You should not be in such an ambiguous position.
There are definitely two worlds in the world. There are wicked people and good people, or true and false. What is the purpose of education? It is to create good people. It is easier to become a wicked person than to become a good person. To become a wicked person, no education is needed.
No education is needed… that itself is simply wicked. It is through education that one can separate from evil; it is through education that one can distinguish between good and evil...
Education and ethics all set the standard for goodness. The path that sets the standard for goodness is not an easy path. It is a path of suffering. Everything my body desires conflicts with the essential nature. 
The path that does not follow this cannot find good results; this is the standard of teaching in our social life today.
From this, we can see that the world is mixed with good and evil. We must remove evil and seek only good. We must discern this. When we see through the lens of what our will desires, what must we discern? The archangel could not fulfill his responsibility as a servant before God, so he could not reach the position where he could give absolute loyalty. To compensate for that, we must absolutely take responsibility for the position of the servant. That is why the Unification Church guides us through this course. When you enter the Unification Church, you must make sacrifices.
"All people hope for good, so before serving God, serve people. For the sake of all humanity. Love people. Live for people. You were born for people." This is the education we must receive. You were not born for yourself. If you were born for yourself, you cannot discern the path of the restoration of the archangel. Do you understand? If it is a position for oneself, then as fallen humans, we must discern that the archangel brought about the fall by not serving humanity, and we cannot find the way to compensate for this.
Then, what has the position of the son been until now? It is not the true son of God. It is the position of an adopted son. You must understand this. It is an adopted son, an adopted son. What is an adopted son? It is one with a different bloodline. It has started from a different father. This is how it is. Due to the fall, today’s humanity is in a position similar to that of an adopted son. What caused us to become adopted sons? It was because of Satan. Therefore, in order for the adopted son to be restored, what must be done? We must subdue the son who represents Satan. We must substantiate the archangel type. This is the path desired by the will.
The difference between Cain and Abel
Therefore, the issue of Cain and Abel always remains. When there are two people, they cannot both be the same. If a purpose is established centered around the two, it will definitely be centered around a good person. Among the two, the one who is slightly better stands in the Abel-like position corresponding to a slightly better field.
As that field grows, it becomes a larger Abel. Thus, individual Abels arise among Abels, and there arise Abels representing families. This is how it grows. There are tribal Abels among Abels, there are national Abels among Abels, and there are world Abels that arise. On the opposing side, individuals arise, opposing families arise, opposing nations arise, and opposing worlds arise.
Therefore, at the end, the world will definitely be divided into two. When it becomes two and the time comes for "I am right. I am right," know that it is the end! Know that it is the end!
When we look at Cain and Abel, as the day of judgment approaches, Cain will make excuses in his own way, and Abel will defend himself in his own way. Therefore, the time will come when they reveal themselves. The time will come to discern who is right and who is wrong. For that, they will clash. They will clash. Then, how can we know Cain? How do the characters of Cain and Abel differ? Standing in the right position is Abel, while standing in the position of striking is Cain. You must understand this.
When we look at the world today, who stands in the position of striking? It is the communist world, and who stands in the position of being struck? It is the democratic world. If we look at one nation, in a democratic world, those who do not believe in religion stand in the position of striking, while those who believe in religion stand in the position of being struck. It is the non-believers who criticize the believers. It is not the believers who criticize the non-believers; rather, it is the non-believers who criticize the believers. The non-believers persecute and criticize the believers. That is how it is, right?
Therefore, in discerning Cain and Abel, what is right is Abel, and what strikes is Cain.
After striking and being struck, if a final resolution is reached, both sides will be exhausted. They will be exhausted. If both fight to the end, both will perish. That cannot happen. One of them must inevitably perish. One of them must inevitably yield. That is how it is. Then, which one will yield? The wicked one will yield first. Why? Because the wicked one has opposed but feels the pangs of conscience. Right? They may boldly come forward to make excuses and defend themselves, but when faced with the truth, they feel the pangs of conscience saying, "You rascal!" Because they feel the pangs of conscience, the consumption of conscience occurs. Do you understand? However, the person standing in the right position, who does not feel the pangs of conscience, will revive more and more as the opposition intensifies. Instead of feeling pangs of conscience, they will actually experience growth. Right? 
When the wicked strike, the more they strike, the stronger Abel becomes. Conversely, those who strike become weaker. Therefore, goodness remains, and evil? It perishes.
However, today, the democratic world does not realize which side it stands on. This is a problem. They do not know whether they stand on the side of good or the side of evil. The day they realize they stand on the side of good, they can say, "I have God on my side, and since I stand on the side of good, strike as you wish." They become stronger. The more they strike, the closer our side gets to God. That is how it is. Isn’t it? When an older brother who has done wrong strikes a younger brother in front of their parents, the parents will inevitably side with the younger brother, even if they do not want to.
It is the same principle. You must clearly understand which side you stand on, but because you are confused, when you get hit once, you say, "Yeah, yeah," and that is confusion. When you know what is right and stand firm, God will inevitably be on your side.
However, today, Christianity has not been able to stand in a position to assert what is right until the end. That is confusion. An Abel is not someone who lives for his own will until death. Right? Jesus also did not live for His own will until death. "Abba, Father! Not my will, but Yours be done. Father, why have You forsaken me? Even if You forsake me, I will not forsake You." He clearly understood. He had a firm conviction that he had the true will.
But what about today? The environment that confronts us, or the persecution of enemies...
This burden, even if it increases, is not a problem. It is certain to lead to destruction. It would be a serious issue if the democratic world does not hold this belief. On the contrary, the communist world possesses the conviction that "if we strike, it will fail." Ideologically, they elevate their beliefs and confidently assert, "If we strike, it will fall to our bat." This is the nature of the communist party. If it is correct, it is bound to fail, but the reason it does not perish is that it can confidently claim the authority of a parent and receive the protection of a parent. Because there are no people who can boast of having such authority as a son, Christianity is deteriorating today, and the democratic world is weakening.

In other words, they are not in a position to inherit the father's will as sons. This is the problem. If one becomes aware of this and stands confidently as the son of the father, then today’s communist world will collapse. They strike up to three times. They strike once, strike twice, and that is why we go through the patterns of World War I, World War II, and World War III.

It is an era of striking the body, followed by an era of striking the heart, an era of striking affection, and then an era of striking God. This is how it develops.

Until now, it has been a struggle to seize the body. If we look closely at human history, what have wars been fought for until now? They were fought to seize land. It is a struggle to seize land. Land symbolizes the body, right? "Yes." Then what is the next struggle to seize? The next is a struggle to seize people centered on the ideology of the Lord. Right? What is the next struggle to seize? It is a struggle to unify everything centered on who becomes the master. That is the struggle. The communists are currently engaged in that game. They are using force to unify around communist ideology. Love the party. Love the party. You must love the party more than your wife and children, right? What is that party? If Kim Il-sung is the husband, then the party is like the wife. The party is Kim Il-sung's house. That is how it is. It is Kim Il-sung's house. To become one is similar to direct descendants.

The world of Satan has gone to such an extent that it focuses on people and concentrates them in one place to strike whom? It strikes God. Did it strike God? "Yes." It is a struggle to seize the body, heart, and people, and then it seeks to take away all love from humanity. After that, the communists strike even God.

We must center ourselves on God and align our bodies with God, align the hearts of humanity with God, and ideologically encompass humanity to bring them to God. After that, we must gather love in God's house centered on God and make it so that we cannot oppose God at all. When we look at this historical development, you must understand that this is an inevitable result.

Without Cain and Abel becoming one, restoration cannot happen.

What is the path that the will desires? We must find the path to complete as the archangel, and then we must find the path to complete as adopted sons. It is adopted sons, adopted sons. In the path of adoption, there is Cain. Cain must be subdued. Without subduing Cain, it cannot be done. Only by subduing Cain and becoming one can we enter the position to receive the son. What is the son? He is the parent of humanity. He is the Messiah. In other words, without the restoration of Cain and Abel, there is no way to save Adam. You must understand this. The principle is set that way, right?

Abel is for the restoration of the parents, for the restoration of Adam and Eve. Restoration cannot be done alone. Cain and Abel must become one, and only when they appear as true brothers can they meet Adam and Eve, who stood at the stage just before the fall and did not fall.

What is that Adam and Eve? They are the bridegroom and bride. This is how it is. By receiving that bridegroom and bride and becoming one with God's love, we can inherit the position of true parents and finally become good ancestors. This is the path of restoration. Consequently, the completion of the realm of the son-in-law occurs. When that realm of the son-in-law is completed, what happens next? There must be three archangels. This is how it is. Therefore, in the Unification Church, to receive the blessing, there must be three children of faith, right? "Yes." When viewed from the perspective of relative ideology, it becomes Noah's eight family members. It is all like that.

What is God's desired will? What is the path that the will desires? It is simple. You yourselves must restore the archangel through indemnity. After that, you must restore the path of adoption through indemnity. Then you must enter the direct bloodline of the adopted son. That is to receive the Messiah and be grafted in.

I mentioned this when a student came recently, but you must enter the direct bloodline of God as an adopted son. To enter, it is not simply done as it is. You must go through all the laws of indemnity. The process is complicated. Without going through that process, you cannot get married. Do you understand what I mean? If you get married without going through that process, it becomes like a fertilizer factory that breeds Satan's offspring. It is nothing more than a factory producing Satan. It has nothing to do with God's sons and daughters. You must go through this process. You must be grafted in.

After being grafted in, you must be completely united with the sap of that original tree. Without standing in that position, you cannot walk the path of restoration. You must understand that. Therefore, you must restore as a servant, and then restore as an adopted son, and then? At the same time as you take the position of a direct son, you must also take the position of the bridegroom. What comes next? After that, you must become one with God. You become one with God. 

You must give birth to sons and daughters who can make God rejoice, united with God's love. This is the completion of the realm of the son-in-law. Isn't it?

What is the will? That is the will. If Adam and Eve were there, that would be the end of it. However, when we look at our fallen humanity today, in front of the will, your individual family is at stake, and then? The nation is at stake, and then? The state is at stake, and then the world is at stake. Do you understand? This is the thought.

Therefore, individual restoration alone will not suffice. A tradition must be established that can go all the way back to restore the individual, family, tribe, nation, state, and world to be able to welcome the Messiah. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That is how it is. Therefore, in our Unification Church, we say that only after completing individual restoration, family restoration, national restoration, and world restoration can we complete the restoration of the cosmos. The spiritual world and the physical world will finally be completed. This is why it is thought, this is why.

Did Abel truly die while centering on the historical original hope? Did he die saying, "Father, my death is for the sake of your future will, to pioneer the hope you desire, to sow the seed"? Did he think, "Even if I die, dying in a position where I can do that is a valuable death"? That is the question.

Looking at Grandpa Noah, who toiled for 120 years, if he spent those 120 years from the perspective of "I toil for the sake of the will and to leave behind more valuable content for the future," then that life would indeed be a life that remains in history. However, if he thought, "I have toiled for 120 years to build the ark so that I alone can be saved," without considering God's future will, then he would not be a person suitable for the original intention that God had chosen and established.

If Noah himself, upon coming down from the ark, had thought, "I lived this life for God's will, and even after coming down from the ark, I live all things to glorify God's future will," then wouldn't there have been no history of resentment? That is the issue. Did all of Noah's toil for 120 years truly serve the future world of God's will? Did he align with God's desired wish and look forward to the future world that God wants to find and hopes for every day? When we ask this, we cannot say that it was all so. What about Abraham? Wasn't he the same?

When God blesses such people, He should teach them, "You will become the ancestor of a superhuman faith in the future world. Your descendants will become super-national and super-national ancestors in the future." However, looking at what He taught our ancestors repeatedly, didn't He always emphasize "your descendants"? "Your descendants will multiply like the stars in the sky and the sand on the earth." Ultimately, the emphasis on "you" raises the question of whether it is God's original will to emphasize the individual or whether the original intention is to emphasize that "you" should represent the world and be for the sake of the world and all humanity. 

When we consider the emphasis on "you," it seems to reflect the weakness of humanity, which cannot escape from itself. Looking at Abraham, why did our ancestors repeatedly make mistakes during important times, such as when offering sacrifices? It is because they always had the habit of thinking centered on the concept of self. Due to that habit and tradition, even though they bore the responsibility of God's restoration providence, they failed to fulfill it.

The same goes for Moses. Moses, representing the Israelite nation, should have thought that even when he faced loneliness or difficulties, it was not for his own sorrow but for the sorrow of the nation and the world. He should have walked the path of sorrow on behalf of God's past sorrow and misery, believing that by walking this sorrowful path, he could remove that sorrow and prevent further sorrow. Therefore, hurry and stretch out your hand to scratch. Am I not in a position to scratch the radius of the earth?" Think like this. It must be different.  
Even when walking the path, think, "I embrace the world beyond the nation, heaven and earth, hear my words." At that moment, I am a public being. When you step out like that, millions of people will be swept in without knowing it. Do you understand?  
You must understand that bowing your head before a sacrifice is the principle. Do you understand? Become a sacrifice. There is no way to perish by becoming a sacrifice. The place where a true sacrifice is offered does not perish. At the end of the sacrifice comes blessings. Isn't that so? You must understand this.

The work I have done is just that much; I cannot fall short of my elder brother. I will overcome the path of greater hardships and globalize the stage. When this traditional spirit overflows in the hearts of the youth, the Unification Church can develop infinitely. Saying, "Oh, since the elders are resting, we should do the same," is a path to ruin. It will lead to ruin.

If it is not the will of heaven to perish, nor the fate of heaven to perish, then that will be fulfilled even if it means abandoning this nation and moving to another country. If that happens, it is the intention that was to be passed on to the people of the Republic of Korea, but it will be inherited by foreign nations. The people of Israel and Judaism should have inherited that, but did not the people of foreign nations inherit Christianity instead? It is the same.

For that reason, you should become people who are remembered in the hearts of the Unification Church members. Do you understand? "Yes." If you have received an award, you must confront national organizations afterward, right? That is how it is meant to be.

Follow such principles and become those who can be remembered in the teacher's heart. What does it mean to be remembered in the teacher's heart? If the teacher is currently fulfilling a national mission and you say, "Oh, I will just focus on my family mission," will you be in the teacher's heart or not? That is a hindrance that follows behind.

To be in the teacher's heart, in an era that urges the national restoration mission, you must become someone who can take responsibility for the nation and the world to come, running directly toward heaven with a sincere heart, day and night. Such a person will surely be remembered in the teacher's heart. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

After completing the national mission, we must go out into the world.

You should pray, "God, my strength is lacking, so please help me," to go beyond the nation and for the world, right? Isn't that so?

The value of the couple that Adam loved is the central value of the world.

Now, our young ladies are graduating. In the world, there may be young women who are about to get married. Why do they get married? It is not for themselves. Why do they get married? They marry to inherit the lineage of countless ancestors and for the sake of future generations. Have you thought about that? They do not marry for themselves. Shouldn't the world love like this? If I die seeing how the father loves, there will be no grievance." You should be able to say this, and if I cannot do it, then let my sons and daughters do it; if my sons and daughters cannot do it, let there be someone in another nation who can do it soon, someone who can shed tears longing to see the father. Then you will be those who remain in God's heart.

"I want to see the family you love and die. If I can be in the position where you looked upon me with compassion, where I can be loved together, how happy would that be? If you die for that day, it is not dying for yourself. Do you understand? The teacher is the same. The teacher is also walking that path. Is it not your wish to become a parent who can look upon sons and daughters that the father can boast about and rejoice in? I must be different from the past me and the present me.

If you become like this, hope will rise from the place of despair, and hope will rise even from the place of discouragement! Therefore, I must be different from the past me and the present me.

In today's living stage, you must feel a sense of fulfillment and value. You must seek the true path of a filial child who can comfort the glorious God rather than just serving the God of restoration.

Let us seek the true path of a filial child who can comfort the glorious God.

"I will cross over to the position of a commander who can lead the front lines. Even if I am lacking in age, I am someone who can take that position, so why am I not entrusted with it?" Looking back, if that period had not existed, what would have happened to me? That period has become a good period that can adorn my life and a foundation for inheriting the blessings. Knowing that there is a hopeful path, we must walk this path with such thoughts and fulfill our mission, so that we can surely live as people of heaven and go to that land as people of heaven. Do you understand? "Yes."

Do you understand? "Yes."

When I think that now is more than the past, today is more than yesterday, and tomorrow is more than today, I realize that I must make a new determination when I pick up my spoon in the morning, and when I eat dinner and lie down at night, I must shine brighter than the morning, and I must shine brighter tomorrow than today. If I continue this daily life of determination, pursuing infinite value and being joyful, I understand that I will never perish. To do so, we must know how much of a path of suffering, persecution, and hardship we must walk, and I earnestly ask that we become those who can accept this meaningfully and recognize the value within it. 

I sincerely ask that not even one life falls away, and that we may be meaningful successors or heirs before this nation and this people. The sleeping humanity of the world must be awakened by us, and this nation and this people have a responsibility to be saved by our hands.

3) Those Who Seek

<Prayer> As we welcome October on this last morning, may Your glory, honor, and praise reach from heaven to this earth. 

Beloved Father, who seeks to save the poor people on this earth who are hoping for atonement, please hasten to save humanity according to Your desired will. Please establish this humanity, which is struggling in the valley of death, upon the authority of Your life, so that they may receive Your original, loving nature and infinitely enjoy joy and glory on that day and at that time. 

We acknowledge that we are humans born as descendants of the Fall. Father, who sees that the sins committed individually have affected families, nations, and the world, I hope You will look upon them with Your boundless mercy, compassion, and love and not abandon them. 

Father, please come to these prostrated children and help them recall the past me, clearly define the present me, and prepare a new awareness that can pursue a future that is meaningful and valuable. I believe that at this time, not only here but also all over the nation, the children who are scattered are fighting to go against the sorrowful path of restoration that You have left behind, and I believe they have come before You, prostrating themselves with their bodies that have been battered. 

Please look upon them and help them become true sons and daughters who can embody the image You desire. 

Father, please do not abandon the nations and peoples that are connected to each of us. To do so, we must recognize that the environment we are connected to is not the problem; rather, we ourselves are the problem. Each person must stand in their position, taking responsibility for themselves, and without self-control and adjustment, we cannot connect the environment that You desire. When we think about this, we cannot help but acknowledge that we are fallen descendants who cannot pursue the value of any object. 

Therefore, You must be the subject here, and please determine my current position where I can pursue the value of the object regarding Your will. When we think that we cannot receive the grace of redemption and the grace of liberation except by being held by Your purpose and the touch of Your power, we cannot help but feel how pitiful You are. 

We know that You must take responsibility for and manage this fallen humanity. We have learned through history and through the Unification Church that there are obstacles of suffering and indemnity that must be crossed to reach the place You desire. 

The more we experience how difficult it is to love heaven and follow heaven's will, the more we realize how miserable the mission You bear to lead such individuals to the nation You desire is. 

Father, have there been any times in historical eras when our ancestors sympathized with the countless times You have called back the people who have betrayed heaven with a compassionate heart? We did not realize how great Your loneliness, misery, and sorrow were every time the one child You found after countless hardships betrayed You. 

It was the same in Adam's family, and the fight between Cain and Abel brought about such results. In the 120 years of suffering endured by Grandfather Noah, such a day was also met. In the journey of Abraham's household, while seeking the place of blessing, the desired altar of blessing was set, yet such results came about. We know that even Moses, who spent his entire life in the kingdom of Egypt for the sake of the Israelite people, faced such days of sorrow. 

Throughout the 4,000 years of historical processes leading up to the time of John the Baptist and Jesus, many of our ancestors carried the historical mission, yet there were not many who held onto Your heart, Your circumstances, and Your desires while struggling for humanity. 

When we think about this, we realize how hard it must have been for You, and how many times You must have wanted to express the mixed feelings hidden within those circumstances. While humans could pray to You to relieve their own sorrows, You had no one to appeal to when You were sorrowful. We must truly come to know You. 

There are many Christians scattered around the world, but when we consider how rare it is for those who love Your heart, Your circumstances, and Your desires, and who struggle centered on Your heart, circumstances, and desires, we realize that only Jesus knew Your heart. 

"Abba Father, not my will, but Yours be done!" Jesus, who knew that even if He walked the path of death, You should not suffer the pain of death, was the only true son who could share Your heart. 

How wonderful it would have been if that son had a family, a tribe, a nation, and a world to comfort You, but that son could not leave behind a foundation on this earth to comfort You. That son should have had the position to love individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, yet he did not have such a position. 

The Jewish community, which had been prepared for 4,000 years, longed to welcome the Messiah and serve him, but when he spent thirty years on this earth, who among them truly longed for him or sought to serve him? We must recognize this miserable fact that not a single person was there. 

Even the beloved twelve apostles, during the three years of suffering, did not know the sorrow of the nation or the painful heart of the denomination that Jesus carried on behalf of heaven. The days they faced were sad days, and the things they endured were persecution. They did not understand that the one who had to bear Your circumstances and heart, and fulfill Your desires, was the Son of God, the Prince of God. 

Although there was no one to serve Jesus at that time, many have come to believe in the exalted Jesus through the course of history. When we think about how many people shed blood in sacrifice and how many tragic events occurred in the history of martyrdom leading up to the exaltation of Jesus, we realize that there was a horrific blood history that continued behind the history of the coming Jesus. 

We understand that it was not Your will to send Jesus to see this. We also recognize that You are not a God who rejoices in the fact that the history of salvation is achieved through such paths of death and bloodshed. When we think about this, we realize how pitiful You are, advancing the history of liberation and salvation through misery, loneliness, and lamentation. 

Father, when we think about the fact that we must become those who can comfort such a Father, we cannot help but feel the profound pain of the distant, sorrowful cross. 

Father, we did not know that such a mission remains in the historical purpose. Now that we know this content and look up to heaven, we find that we have no strength to pray for anything before heaven. We only hope for the time when we can participate in Your sorrow with tears and prostration, and we can only wish to reach the limit of overcoming on Your path of suffering. 

However, knowing that there is an inseparable story and connection between You and us, we must call upon You, seek You, and follow the path You take. As You look upon our steps, which walk without knowing the path of suffering, we see that You cannot abandon us, nor can You curse and remove us. 

Father, how many times must Your story have been more pitiful than our personal situations, and how many times have You labored from a place of concern that far exceeds the concerns of individuals throughout our lives? We must become those who can at least think about this in our hearts. 

Even so, when we think about how You still have the path to hold onto and labor for these people, we must not leave any appearance of unfaithfulness before You, who desires to remove evil and walk the path of goodness. 

Through this moment today, we struggle with loneliness, with sighs, and with a heart that wants to care for You and serve You. 

Father, I thank You for leading us this far, and as I realize that behind the Unification Church, which has come to this day, there is a path of suffering that no one knows, I feel once again that I am unworthy before You. 

If the Unification Church had not appeared on this earth, it would not have increased the burden of Your labor, but because the Unification Church has appeared, I know well that You have faced the path of loneliness for 27 long years since liberation, and You have encountered sorrow. 

The members of the Unification Church, who should comfort that sorrow, are still following the habit of reporting their own sorrows to You, and I hate myself for still carrying that sorrow. I wish to discover a self that can deeply sense the appearance that can bring joy to You. 

This place may be humble, but it is the headquarters that the Unification members admire and look upon. It is the center. When the center goes wrong, the whole collapses. The mission to uphold the center lies with the members of the Unification Church, and since the center we must serve is You, we realize that the entire membership has the responsibility to unite and uphold You. Only then can that center stand forever.
The more I think about being preserved, the more I realize that we must become a group of people who can uphold and establish ourselves centered on the will of heaven in every possible way. Regardless of what others say, whether they call us heretics or rebels, if you become the rightful heir who can remember the bloodline that you have inherited, then there is no greater wish than that. At this time, I earnestly ask you, Father, to encourage the family of unification who knows this well. If the battleground of your fight remains, please stir them up from within. Direct them to the battlefield they must go to, so that they can prepare their whole life with one heart and mind, and become a strong and courageous army of heaven, capable of taking on the responsibility of heavenly soldiers and going into action.

Now we have said that we are going for your nation. We have said that we are going for the resting place where you can find peace. We have come to understand that we must find a home where you can rest. My staying here is for the purpose of finding a home where you can rest. Our wish is to go out seeking a nation where you can reign, and we have come to know that this is also your wish. 

It is your wish that this world be restored to a world governed by you, and we have come to understand that we are in a desperate situation, bearing the heavy burden of the cross to fulfill that wish. When I think of the profoundly noble heart of the Father’s sacrifice that underpins this desperate situation, we too must be like that. Our path of hope and purpose is to liberate this world. 

Our situation is to carry the cross that remains in this world, and the limit we must overcome is to lead them with the bonds of love, even if it means facing death. When I think of this as the foundation of our hearts, if we have become poor souls who are struggling to become a group of filial piety that can take on the Father’s responsibility and reduce this in our daily lives, then I know that such a person will not perish. Every time I stand in such a position, I have heard the Father’s encouragement. When I stand in such a position and fight, I have seen that I did not desire the results of victory, but I was met with them. That is why I knew that you are the living Father, and that is why I came to know that you are the accompanying Father.

Father, who cannot forget the Unification Church, please do not forget the heart that sought you with hope, and do not turn back. Until the day of final victory, the day when we offer the final glory and the Holy Spirit, until that day when all nations raise the banner of liberation and all people can praise, if we cannot fulfill our new mission on earth, then even in death, let us become a group of heavenly warriors who bear the burdens of this age and fight. I earnestly hope and wish for this. Father! Please remember the children scattered across the nation. Facing the urgent and pressing responsibility and mission that we must undertake in the midst of the world’s end-time situation, when we think of this, we must look straight at your will, once again emulate the victory path you walked, and earnestly ask that we do not delay in fulfilling the mission of heavenly pioneers who open a new tomorrow.

To the Unification groups scattered around the world, every time we receive letters looking forward to the day we meet again, we know they are pitiful. Even if they are from different ethnicities or have different traditions and customs, as long as we know they are a group walking the path of inheriting the heart of heaven, I earnestly hope and wish that you will protect their suffering, Father. 

Moreover, at this time, please remember the Unification groups fighting underground within the communist realm, holding onto the will of heaven that others do not know. In places where there are groups who are risking their lives and looking forward to serving you freely in their daily lives, I earnestly hope and wish that you will protect them, Father. When I think that you still have the situation where you must guide and encourage them, I feel that you are pitiful.

Father, the Unification Church has gone through an unknown path of suffering until now and has pioneered an unknown world. Father, please extend your hand even to the communist realm. I have come to understand that we are hastening our advance until the day when the banner of freedom is raised high with you, and the Unification groups can lift their hands in praise on the day of victory. I earnestly hope and wish that infinite blessings, mercy, and love will dwell in front of the path that the heavenly sons and daughters who have sacrificed everything in front of your solemn calling take. 

Father, please protect Korea. I can feel the heart of Abraham praying before Sodom and Gomorrah. In front of the heart that hoped that even the last ten would remain, we too wish to have the same heart and hope for this month to be peaceful and understanding. Now, please allow us to break through this three-year journey smoothly, and let the day you wish for come quickly. We must fight without rest. We must make an effort. When I open my eyes and look at the three-thousand-ri peninsula, I have come to understand the bitter resentment that remains for the future of Asia, and that we must overcome and resolve this from a detached position. 

When we look at ourselves, we find ourselves in a living environment that is under threat. This is not only for individuals but also for families, ethnic groups, and nations. Even the United States, which was leading the free world, and the Soviet Union, which was leading the communist world, are in such a situation, and we see this at the present moment. Instead of uniting and cooperating to pioneer towards the ideal future, there is a rising tide of conflict, disputes, and self-assertion, with little room for compromise. Given this, we cannot see that the path this world is taking is leading to happiness for humanity today.

Therefore, we can conclude that this world, the current situation, stands in a position that is utterly disconnected from the will of heaven, if heaven exists. If religion has taken on the mission of adjusting this current world to a new path, it must digest this and lead it in a new direction. However, instead of doing that, it has become a phenomenon of being dragged along by the world rather than leading it. By becoming secularized, religion has naturally diminished the possibility of fulfilling the path of desire that God wished to achieve through this secularized religion. Therefore, even if God exists, we cannot help but feel that he cannot abandon this world or distance himself from it.

For this reason, if God is to move away from the religion that was centered on him, it will lead to a situation where the further away God moves, the more the religion he guided becomes secularized and faces corruption alongside the world. This is an inevitable conclusion that we cannot ignore. 

If that is the case, where is the path that must be taken to reach the world through religion? If the path to find that way begins, then surely God, who has been nurtured behind religion until now, will manifest. If the religion that has been believed and nurtured until now stands in a position to be rejected by God due to unfilial or unfaithful results, then if there are groups that take on the path of filial piety or loyalty in a new aspect, it is only natural to think that they can propose a new movement that can love God in this aspect while abandoning the former. If there is a place where this can happen, and if there is any denomination that can follow this path and inherit God's will, we can conclude that there is a possibility of developing a new historical movement on a global scale through that denomination.
However, when we think about it at that moment, is there really such a denomination, such a religion on this earth? We are unable to discover what exists. If God exists, it is only natural that He should leave behind a religious foundation through which He can reconcile this world that has fallen into evil. However, when we ask if there are groups that can pursue what can be left behind, we realize that it is hard to find such groups. In other words, today, something new must emerge before the established religions. We must break away from this old system and present a movement for innovation. This applies not only to Christianity but also to many other religions.

As you know, when we look at the religious landscape centered around the small territory of Korea, it is clear that the religions that have existed until now are not sufficient. We must either cut it off, break it apart, or shatter it, and under a new unity, a new movement for innovation must arise. This conclusion cannot be denied, as it is accompanied by the threats in your daily life and the worries that seep in at every moment, leaving a yearning for this.

In a time of global despair, God is seeking people. Therefore, if we have lost God, we are in a position of loss, and if humanity has strayed from the path of its uncorrupted nature, we are in a state of deviation. If there is a God, it is time for religion to seek Him again, and humanity on this earth must find a way to return to being human. However, by human power alone, we cannot find a way to do so, and there is no solution that can be resolved by human strength. We are at a point where humanity must once again examine the lives and paths they have walked, as we have collided with the end where no hope remains possible with human strength. In other words, we must turn back because something has gone wrong if we continue as we are. Religion has compromised and sought after the world until now, but it has gone wrong because the world is wrong. We must review it again, both externally and internally, and make a new decision. This decision should not center around a specific denomination but should seek a direction that combines global religions. Furthermore, the decision should not be made based on a single nation but must be made collectively by the nations of the world.

Thus, can we conclude that this is the end for religion and the end for the world? Will God leave us, who are in such a position, to our own devices? Will God abandon this world that stands in such a position? If God exists, He cannot abandon us. Because He cannot abandon us, God will seek out those who can help. Who are those people? They must not be those who have become weary and fallen behind in this world, disappearing with the final cries of despair, but rather those who can rise again with a new determination amidst despair. They must be religious individuals who, instead of being engulfed in despair and lamenting over corrupt religions, break through and present a new tomorrow.

If religious people cannot awaken to this and if the people of the world awaken first, then this may be the time when God will choose the people of the world over religious individuals. We cannot help but think this way. Therefore, if God exists, He will seek people. What kind of people does God seek? Not those who lament in despair, but those who can break through, plan for tomorrow, and possess the driving force to infinitely resolve these issues with strong and courageous hearts. It is a valid conclusion that there may be such groups among those whom God seeks.

As you know, when Moses, who led the people of Israel, was about to die, God entrusted Moses' mission to Joshua and Caleb, saying that the path ahead is one of struggle, and the land of Israel they must go to is the land of Canaan, which the people of Israel could not enter even after killing their own. God, knowing this, placed these two young men before the nation and commanded them to "be strong and courageous." No matter how difficult the circumstances may be, do not become a man who is pushed back by those circumstances. Your conviction must come first. Even if the nation rebels, your conviction must surpass that rebellious nation. We know this fact.

In the same way, God is surely seeking. If God were dead, we would not know, and if there were no God, we would not know either, but there must be a place where He is seeking. That place is not where we are groaning in a state of despair and worry, but a place that holds the hope of overcoming that despair. How wonderful it would be if we could hope for a tomorrow that is better than today! If there is a way to do that, everyone can smoothly go that way at once. However, if that is not the case and we turn around to live, all conditions for the future would welcome us, and we could spend our lives joyfully, but that is not the case. To overcome that, we must either prepare for death and seek new solutions, or we must think about how to return to the historical point where we have walked until now, resolving all historical matters.

We must recognize that the path to overcoming and transcending this is to leap beyond these circumstances, and there are only two ways: either to leap over them or to leap over them before starting. There is no other solution. No matter how much one groans within this, a person who has fallen into a sewer will only sink deeper the more they struggle. Therefore, a leap is necessary here. We must have the conviction that we can overcome this and firmly establish the foundation for tomorrow's victory, or we must seek the way to return to that historical point because what we have done until now is wrong. 

Why? Because through countless lives, countless intellectuals, and countless efforts, the results have reached a point where they cannot stop. When we look at this, to leap over it, we must either completely resolve the present or allow anyone to go as they please. If that is not possible, we are in a position to be left behind as the debris that is being dragged in while dying, which is why we are taught to transcend this.

The path of religion has always been a path of pursuit. Religion has always played such games. It has not taught us to serve God while living a comfortable life in this world. It has always called us to overcome and transcend. Therefore, religions like Buddhism have completely abandoned the world and turned away from the path that humanity takes. We know that this has been repeated. In contrast, Christianity has contributed to the historical era while standing behind the forefront of modern civilization. It has compromised with the world and infiltrated it. Yet, standing in the midst of this, it has imposed a negative mindset rather than a positive one. The saying in the Bible, "Those who seek to save their lives will lose them, and those who lose their lives will save them," is all paradoxical and contradictory. Therefore, rather than making a resolution to die, it has come to make a resolution to die in order to live. Only from there can we discover a new path of overcoming, and we must recognize that this was the last serious word that Jesus could not help but say to His beloved disciples.

Thus, there will be people whom God seeks. Who are those people? Must they have strong and courageous convictions to be found? No. They must have strong and courageous convictions, but they must also have a purpose. The words God spoke to Joshua and Caleb to be strong and courageous carry the meaning of "You must restore tomorrow's Israel." It is a call to return to the land of Canaan. The purpose of going towards the land of Canaan must be clear. It is on this clear foundation that we must be strong and courageous. That is what is needed.

In today's path of religion, is the purpose clear? It is vague. For example, in Christianity, people say they believe in Jesus to go to heaven, but human purpose cannot end there. Look. When someone says, "I will go to heaven by believing in Jesus," who will go? "I will go. I will go to this place." This is a position that forsakes everything. It is a position of losing everything. Isn't that so? When someone says, "I will believe in Jesus and send my family to heaven," it is a position where they can find their family, but when they say, "I will believe in Jesus and go to heaven," when they say, "I will go," it means they would forsake their family if they have one.

The essence of religion must be analyzed once again. Today, Christianity has all subjective standards of faith, and among those, are there people who believe, saying, "I will do this for the sake of saving a greater nation"? When we delve into the essence of faith, there are those who shed blood, sweat, and tears for their own salvation, but are there those who walk the path of death for the sake of sending their nation to heaven? Have there been people who said, "Let us believe in Jesus to establish heaven in the world. Let us believe in Jesus to lead the world to heaven"? Can that world be established without including me? The nation is established by combining each individual. 

However, even when we look at the believers of Christianity today, when they say, "Let us go to heaven," who will go? "Let me go." Therefore, when we see their prayers, they only pray for "my sons and daughters..." They only seek their own religion. This denomination only seeks its own church. Whether it is Presbyterian or Methodist... all of this must be shattered. It is all wrong. If there is a God, would He be pleased with that? Let us speak frankly. What is God's will? "Kim, you alone seeking is God's will." Is that so? Then what will happen when you believe in Jesus? "I will go to heaven." When will you go to heaven? You say you will go when you die, which is a one-way ticket. If you go while alive, after you have been saved, you could return, and if you went to heaven, then if it is good, you could bring others back, but you say you will go when you die, which is a one-way ticket for everyone. This faith concept is flawed, isn't it? Such a religion does not need God. If I were God, I would blow it away.

If you live in one house but only want to eat well and do well for yourself, will you not be driven out of that family? A child who should take care of their parents but only wants to eat well is being unfilial, unfilial.

You do not understand what position an individual can occupy here. You have forgotten that. What is the position an individual should stand in? An individual should stand above the nation. An individual should stand above the world. Therefore, is not the desire of humanity to become the number one in the world? Isn't that so? You must understand that.

When we ask our youth, "If you succeed in the future, what will you become?" no matter how incompetent they are, they will say, "Ah! I will become the president of this country." Their hearts are all like that. However, that is a foolish person. "Are you satisfied being the president of one country? You should aim to be the president of the world." Their ambition is greater than the earth. Not only greater than the earth, but also greater than God. Therefore, they can live with God in their hearts while being arrogant. They even try to put God inside them. Do you not have such ambition? The position where a person can stand is not to stand above themselves. It is to stand in a place where something greater, like heaven, is already being spoken of in relation to the whole earth, where one can stand in a position of leading the people. One must be a person who can receive the welcome of heaven to enter heaven; can someone who cannot be welcomed in heaven say, "I will go to heaven"? What nation would there be for such a person? They are alone. Such a heaven is not heaven.

When you go to the spiritual world, you will find that those who were once great figures in the Old or New Testament, respected and martyred, are in the most miserable places. Those who thought, "I must die like this to go to heaven," cannot go to heaven. Those who died like that have the mindset similar to that of someone who committed suicide for heaven due to madness. However, in contrast, there are those who did not become martyrs but endured hardships while believing, saying, "Ah! I will sacrifice myself to make the nation a heaven and lead many people to heaven." Such a person is in heaven.

We must reform the essence of faith. Because Christianity has held such thoughts, many storms have arisen. The thought of the Unification Church is to break through these storms. It will collapse without needing to be broken. But why must it be broken quickly? Because if it collapses, it will all be forsaken before God, and that is why we must break it down to save it. That does not mean to break it down with an axe.

Instead of saying, "Let us believe in Jesus and go to heaven," we should say, "Let us believe in Jesus, establish heaven, and when that heaven is established, we will go to the heavenly kingdom." This is the normal direction of faith that God desires, isn't it? Saying, "Whether the nation collapses or the world collapses, I can go to heaven," is foolishness. Do we feed such pastors? Before long, they will be expelled before the Unification Church. It will surely happen. Before long, they will be thrown into a pit by the young believers they raised. This will inevitably happen. This is not a threat. Whether pastors are here or not, it will definitely happen.

The Unification Church advocates a more public faith. In this respect, our Unification Church has a representative faith. It aims to break down religions that are ruining history and collapsing with the world, to create heaven, and to make people who can be sent to God and to the heavenly kingdom according to that created heaven. Even if there is one believer, would not such a person be favored? "My church," whose church is that? Who is the church of the general assembly? Who is the church of the bishop? Not a chance. These wicked groups.

From now on, we must attack. Starting from the day after 1972, we must attack the established churches. We are not in a position to lose if we confront them with power. We have the autonomous capability to push them back in any way. Let’s see who wins. God will judge fairly.
