At some point, when faced with a serious situation that determines life and death, we must seek Your agreement and be willing to accept the rebuke You give us, knowing that this is the path of fallen people. Therefore, today, the members of the Unification Church are serious people.

We must be crazy about loving humanity, crazy about fulfilling the will, and we must cry out desperately to receive Heaven's cooperation while confessing our weak lives to You. We should not be ashamed of what anyone says. No matter what anyone says about the path of following You, even if they comment on our insignificant and shabby appearances, the path of looking to You is the path of hope, and the path of following You is the inevitable path we must take. Therefore, knowing this inevitability, we must run toward the serious days where we cannot see our shabby appearances or the scorn of our environment.

Father, when those who have called upon You and sought You become exhausted and fall, how pitiful must You be, as You cannot abandon them? You must stop Your busy steps and look upon us, hoping for our awakening. We must always be awake. We must always be awake. You have told us not to cease praying. You have told us to pray while awake. In the end, we must anoint our heads with oil and enter the secret place to pray. When asked for whom we should pray, we must pray for Heaven. We must pray to meet You. We must realize that this body, which does not become one with Your love, must pray even through sleepless nights to find that connection.

Father, how much have we truly felt the fact that we have fallen? Am I not in a position where I must navigate my fate in a desolate desert, where the sandstorm blows and I cannot see ahead or behind? Now, where shall I go? The further I go, it seems there is no path of hope, only a path of despair. How grateful I would be if a shining morning star appeared in the eastern sky to illuminate my path! If not, whether it be a form or a symbol, it would be good to hear Heaven's voice calling me to come, or how happy it would be to have the day when You directly appear to guide our path! We must understand that such things do not happen until our earnest hearts, which long to cross the line of life and death, become deeply rooted in that center. We must reflect on the fact that we cannot hope for the life of Heaven beyond our own death.

Now, I, who am caught in suffering and must leave behind a desperate lament with my fate, even if I rely on someone, I realize that I am relying on something as worthless as a rotten stick. How painful it is, how anxious, and how helpless it feels to long for life without having experienced such struggles and experiences. Father, is it not Your wish that we be driven toward the narrow valley, toward the path that can lead to the final destination?

Father, please do not abandon us. Where Your hand is present, there is hope, and we know that there is no despair in following the footsteps You have left behind. Therefore, each of us must connect with You in the depths of our lives, and our wish must be to anticipate the place where the realities of Your movement can manifest in our living environments. Father! We earnestly hope and desire that You hold onto us.

Now, November and December are approaching, and so is 1973. As each year passes, we must become those who understand how frightening it is that the appointed time for restoration and indemnity comes as a time of lamentation rather than joyful days.

The year 1972, which we emphasized as a historic year, is almost over, with only 60 days remaining. The world situation has changed, but the circumstances in Korea have also changed. Even though the Unification Church must change to fulfill one purpose, if it has not changed, we must realize that it is broken and wrong.

We must change our hearts more than we change outwardly. Our hearts must be filled with earnestness. We must have a strong conviction that we must go even if it means dedicating our lives to fulfill the will. We must feel regret and sorrow for not being able to dedicate ourselves to You in 1972. When we think that we must spend the remaining time meaningfully, Father, please hold us and protect us in the embrace of love, and do not abandon the heart of compassion that guides us.

When we open our eyes, the nature we see appears the same every time. When we open our eyes, those we have forgotten always remain forgotten. When we look at the countless crowds hastening toward death, we know that there is no one who can have hope.

Standing alone, we must walk the path of Heaven, but we cannot see Heaven. We cannot see nature. We cannot see people. Unless we have a desperate heart that longs to see this invisible world, we cannot look toward Heaven, nor can we follow You directly. We are in a position where we cannot see Heaven. Therefore, Father, please save us. If possible, please lead us.

Did we not assert our own will? We know that Heaven understands how difficult it is for humans to be this way. Please do not abandon us, and even if it means dragging us forcibly, we earnestly hope and desire that You allow us to remain where You wish.

Father, we must live with childlike hearts. A proud heart brings joy to Satan, while a childlike heart brings joy to Heaven. It has been said that unless one becomes like a child, they cannot enter the Kingdom of Heaven.

Isn't it the attitude of a child to call for their mother and father upon waking? Is it not the position of a child to go and come centered around their parents, or to rejoice? They are in a position where they do not know how they are. They simply like what they have when there is something to eat, and they like it when their mother is present. A child is one who likes relative power and relative objects. Is it not the position of a child to care for others, depend on them, and rejoice?

Today, we do not have the heart of a child. The heart that can rejoice centered around parents, the heart that does not go off to enjoy something good alone but comes to report it to the parents and rejoice with them, is what a child is. Even if we do not have that, we must become like naked children.

That is why Jesus said that unless one becomes like a child, they cannot enter the Kingdom of Heaven. Indeed, how much has Heaven longed for such a child, a child they wish to see? How much has Heaven awaited such a childlike appearance?
Purity, as it is, can be filtered and manifested, reflecting in the environment. Isn't that beautiful appearance the form of a child? Is there not someone who looks at an innocent child and curses? No matter how much of an enemy one may be, shouldn't they love the child first and then hate? If a child can be embraced in the place where heaven loves, let us know that even Satan cannot touch this.

We humans are not people who can be embraced in such a mother's arms. We cannot sit on a mother's lap. How happy is the day when we can be embraced in our parents' arms, yet we do not know how much we long for that, and how much it means to be able to boast in our parents' embrace, becoming a child of that love that can never be forgotten in front of our parents' hearts. Please let us know how much our parents long for that appearance and how beautiful that appearance is.

Father, please come to us. This place is the headquarters of the Unification Church. You know that this child standing here is the son responsible for the Unification Church. When I think about it, all the sorrowful things come to my mind. I remember those days that I cannot forget. If the affairs of the world cannot be a stimulus to long for you, and if they cannot be offered as a condition of glory, how miserable would that be? I am grateful just to have survived under your protection until this hour.

Father, I have come to understand that the path we must take is busy. There are many issues that need to be settled before heaven in light of the domestic and international situation. Many people worry about their personal circumstances and lives, but when I see that there are so few who worry about your will, I realize how pitiful you must be. Our Father is indeed a lonely one. We must not become a group that makes that lonely one even lonelier.

Father, this incredible story, even if I cry out loud, cannot reach your story. These inadequate and insufficient things are too lowly to be called your sons and to be thought of as objects of love by you, the Lord of creation.

Father, if I am an undesirable child, please do not look upon me. This is our wish. Knowing our position that it should not be so, when we think that even the things we dislike must be held onto by you, shouldn't you be mocked before our enemies and walk the path of the cross instead? When I think of this, knowing you makes it frightening to call upon you. The more we know you, the greater the fear we feel. We must realize our position where we hesitate to cover our ugly selves that cannot dare to approach you.

Father, now we welcome the first day of November. At this time, Father, we bow our heads together and pray before you. We must make a resolution about what we will leave behind during this 60-day period, and we must renew our determination. Looking back at history, we must not become a subject of ridicule. When we look at the times, we must not become a figure of mockery. When we think of the future we hope for, today's parents must not dislike such a future. Presenting ourselves in such a position before you, we hope that you alone will strip us of our faults and wash us clean, so we earnestly desire and wish for you to embrace us and remember us.

Please remember your children scattered throughout the world, and especially remember the members of the mobilization team who are running at the forefront. Wherever they go, may the hidden secret history of heaven be revealed, and may the manifestation of the living Father be realized there, so that it becomes a holy activity that can block the world of death and sow the seeds of life. When I meet them again, I must not be in a position to scold them. I hope that it will be a time when heaven can greet them with pride and praise.

Father, I hope that everything will be fulfilled as you have determined. I earnestly wish for you to guide us according to your will. We each pledge at this time to walk that path. We swear to dedicate everything and establish the way of filial piety and loyalty. I pray that you remember us and lead us, and I offer this in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Everyone has wishes. No matter how lowly a person may be, they have wishes from their position. And if they have wishes, they wish for those wishes to be fulfilled.

Humans who have not been able to fulfill their wishes
Just as individuals have wishes, so do organizations. When an organization has wishes and declares that it will fulfill those wishes, it means that it is distancing itself from those wishes. Therefore, to fulfill wishes, one must go through a process to find a place where those wishes align. Until that is achieved, the term fulfillment cannot be established.

Even when centered around a nation, that nation also has its desires. The greater the desire, the more difficult it is to achieve that desire. In the process of fulfillment, suffering of varying degrees occurs in proportion to the size of the wish.

In this way, a nation has its wishes, and furthermore, the nations of the world and all of humanity also have their wishes. Unless those humans or the entirety of humanity share a common purpose and walk the same path of wishes, the fulfillment of the wishes of humanity cannot be expected. When viewed from a flat perspective centered on the current era, we can see that they are interconnected.

We must recognize that such flat phenomena have been layered through historical eras. In each era or each year, countless people who stood on that flat line of historical eras must have harbored wishes, from individuals to the entirety of humanity. Has humanity not carried wishes from Adam until now? Then, have those wishes been genuinely fulfilled in a true sense? When we examine the issue of whether wishes have been fulfilled, we understand through principles that they have not been.

When viewed from the path of faith, no matter how much one feels joy on the path of faith, that joy is not eternal. We feel that joy can come and go in an instant.

Then, throughout the process of history spanning thousands of years from our ancestors to the present, did the people of each era, who had wishes, have any who fulfilled those wishes? Of course, there may have been instances where minor issues or limited time frames allowed for the fulfillment of wishes during a lifetime, but has anyone fulfilled the deeper wishes that yearn for the true meaning of life? We know that no one has.

If any standards of fulfillment had remained in the historical eras and their contents were clearly recorded, humanity could have followed that path and reached the end of the wishes that life truly desires. However, because there are no records that teach such a path—meaning that they did not reach the place of those wishes—humans could not achieve such results.

Where does the desire to meet and love each other between men and women come from?
Therefore, today we too must wish again on the same path as those who have come and gone through the historical process. That wish is not a special wish that I alone desire, nor is it a wish that comes from me. It is a common wish from the standpoint of being human.

So what is the wish of the individual? When we look at individual wishes, there are the wishes of men and the wishes of women. What do men and women wish for? It is that men grow as men and women grow as women, and that they hope for marriage, which has been the historical path that men and women have sought. Many people have followed that path as the way of wishes that life can take. Because it cannot be achieved only as a man or only as a woman, the meeting of man and woman is the wish of those individuals. We know that this has remained as the path that ordinary humans have wished for until now, and it is our position to strive to walk that path.

Then what is the purpose of two men and women meeting and wanting to love? Where will the purpose of love reside? For couples, what is the purpose of their love? Do they love hoping that the results will only affect themselves? Do they love intending to keep their love only for themselves? I do not think so. In love, there must be a desire for the results to connect with the whole. Isn't that the children? They do not merely wish to remain as a couple; they hope that love will bear fruit in some form, and that form is children.

Why do they want to leave children? Why do they not settle for just having the closest counterpart to themselves and desire to leave children? When considering whether it is better to have fewer or more children, a person's desire is that whether they stand in a good position or a noble position, the more they consider themselves a valuable existence, the more they want to leave many descendants centered around that valuable existence. That is human nature.

These days, there is talk of birth control and such. In other words, the nature wishes for blood relations centered on families, which are the foundation of human morality, to increase and spread widely in relative environments, yet birth control can be seen as preventing this.

So, when practicing birth control, is the restriction on children because they do not want children? There is no one who does not want children. In wanting children, one must be the same as others. If there is a son, there must also be a daughter. If they have given birth to sons and daughters, they do not settle for that; they desire better sons and daughters. In other words, they wish for sons and daughters who can stand at the center of all other sons and daughters. Isn't that what any parent, even a bad one, truly wishes for their children? Isn't that love? When we consider this issue, it is not that they want to leave children who follow everyone else; rather, it is the parents' heart that wishes for their children to be the best among all people or all sons and daughters.

Furthermore, what are the wishes of those children? Is it not the heart of the children to boast that they have become the best in front of their parents, that they have exceeded what their parents love, and that the reward of their parents' love has been realized in them?

If such families exist, then those families also have their own wishes. What would be the wish of that family? It is not to become a family that has been forgotten or one that has merely existed traditionally, but rather that our family, centered on our couple and our children, would become a model for all families. That is the truth. If they develop their family and become one clan, that clan would wish to be the best among all clans. Isn't this what a nation is? The people of the Republic of Korea wish for the Republic of Korea to be the best among all nations in the world.

Where are all those wishes connected? They do not wish for something lowly; they all wish to be the best. Even if the territory is small and the population is few, the wish of those who make up that nation is for that nation to become the center of all nations. Thus, the development of the world until now has all returned to the conclusion of nations. This is true from a principled perspective.

Why is that so? It is because, centered on that nation, there is a wish for that nation to become the center of the world. While we may not know what kind of nation should be the center of the world, even if it is a hypothetical wish, it is still a wish that such a nation would exist. Therefore, from individuals to the most central position, it is a demand of humanity that connects from the historical eras to the present and even to the eternal future. This is an undeniable fact.

Then what is the ultimate path? When a nation becomes the center of the world, that nation is not one that stands in opposition to the world. That nation is at the top, reflecting the whole, like a tower. Is it not like a nation that stands at the top of that tower?

So what kind of place is that? That place is where all of humanity looks upon. It is a place where, at the same time, humanity can look upon without despair. The more they look, the more joy they feel. It is a place where they not only have hope but also feel joy directly. It is a place that allows them to have an internal connection that can relate to joy. Isn't that a valid place? In other words, it is not just a place that remains as a wish.

Ultimately, the place that has been wished for is not just a place of wishing; it is a place where what has been wished for is realized, and where they can share the fruits of joy with one another. When they remain in such a place, can the whole not rejoice?

In any case, we humans must go to that place. Why is that? Because when we analyze the desires of our hearts, we find that we wish for so much. Therefore, we can conclude that it is an inevitable path of fate for each individual, whether man or woman, to walk that path.

However, you all cannot all go to that place. Then, when a nation goes to that place, there must be a specific person who remains at the top among the people of that nation. What does this mean? At the very top, the entire population of the nation does not stand equally; it is not that all thirty million people stand at the top. Rather, like a pyramid, there is only one person who sits at the very top among the people of that nation.

To stand at the center, in the representative position, there must be one man and one woman. When viewed from the perspective of people, these men and women will become a couple. Even as a couple, they are not a couple who are the same; rather, they are a couple as subject and object. When they are pointed, it does not mean they are sharp. They must be in such a position to be at the top.

So what is at the very top? It is because the subject and object were created in the creation of heaven and earth that the couple must be the final couple who are synthesized and united based on the standard that stands first, positioned like the subject of God in the realm of duality. This is how we see it. Isn't that how it should be?

When we look at a nation, it is also composed of men and women. In the world, it is all composed of men and women.
At the end, what it comes down to is that we will reach the very top as one man and one woman. However, if there are men and women at that peak, when everyone below says, "I am breaking apart right now," it is something that cannot be prevented from collapsing. Therefore, whether it is the world or anything else, it must come together as one and gradually build up from the very bottom. By building up in this way, when we reach the top and draw a clear line around the position centered on the subject of one man, that subject will stand at the center of the whole, in the position of representation, won't it? No matter how high someone is positioned at the top, if they deviate even a step from that center, what is at the top will inevitably collapse. It is bound to crumble. Therefore, it is enough to be a man or a woman who can do that. Isn't that the conclusion that such men and women must exist?

When we look at it this way, what is the end? If God has a historical providence that creates something like a high pyramid, then at the end, we must place such a man and woman at the top of that providence's pyramid. This is not for individuals but for the world, and not only for the world but also for heaven and earth, so that something representing that must appear on the ground. What is that? Thankfully, it coincides with the idea of the Second Coming and the Messiah.

The top of the tower becomes the absolute center of that tower. The family at the top is not a personal family. It is a family for the whole. If that does not exist, the value of the tower as a tower disappears. Nowadays, we see that at the top of all tall towers, there are lights, and that is because airplanes fly around, right? Even if there were no airplanes, it is human desire to want to leave something at the top that can be looked at at any time. That is what I think. Therefore, rather than just putting something sharp like a lightning rod at a high place, we want to place something else there... If one has built a tall tower, they would want to draw attention to the top rather than just looking at the base of that tall tower. Why is that? Because by looking at it, it is said to be high and good. That is human desire. It is not "Oh, it is high and bad," but rather "It is good!"

When you look at a mountain, no matter how beautiful the scenery is, do you look at the bottom of the mountain and say, "Oh, what a beautiful view!"? Even when looking at something like Mount Geumgang, it is because of the uniquely shaped rocks decorated at the top that we look up and open our mouths in awe, saying, "Ah! How wonderful!" There must be something like that; otherwise, even God would have no choice, right?

The top is the absolute center of all towers. It is the center from a position that transcends class. Isn't that so? Even if it is not the center, without it, the existence value of the tower cannot be formed, so while it is at the top, it becomes the absolute center of the tower. This must not tilt. Wouldn't God desire such a thing?

Nations are like small towers. As these small towers are built, God sees that the materials to build a tower are not everywhere. They have gathered as foolish beings, proclaiming a day of your holy victory, and have faced condemnation from the nation and society. They have shed tears in a place of loneliness where they cannot find friends. When we think about how this was because we first understood that it was your will to leave behind the path determined by heaven on this earth, the longer we walk in accordance with that will, the more it must become a shining history.

We must become a subject with such pride, but if we have not been able to do so, it is a shame for heaven. It is the embarrassment of our ancestors throughout history. When we look at the traditional connections that the Unification family has established, we realize that it is an unspeakable tragedy and shame.

Father! Now, I do not want to become a representative man or woman who is pushed away by this shame. The greatest hope that humanity desires.

Our history in the Unification Church is not long. The Unification Church began its journey right after liberation. is derived from God's ideal world that He was creating.

The desire for the absolute victory of the Unification Church is not a desire for my own victory as the leader of the Unification Church. The victory that the Unification Church seeks transcends me, aiming for the victory of families, nations, and ultimately the world.  
The historical resentment that God has felt began with the mistakes of the ancestors of humanity, and since that day, God Himself cannot escape that lamentation. This lamentation began not because of God, but because of beloved children, and we must understand that it is impossible to remove that cause solely through God Himself.  
There cannot be parents who simply accept ungrateful children. The determination of a filial child cannot be made by parents, no matter how great they are. Similarly, even if God is the absolute owner of the power to create all things, there is no way for Him to escape the sorrow of having to deal with ungrateful children who have left behind a history of lamentation before Heaven.  
Therefore, we must surely go forward.  
Thus, it is certain that God's purpose in seeking true sons and daughters who can liberate Him from the realm of lamentation is to carry out the providence of salvation. In other words, the day must come when God can face the entire universe with joy.  
When God can smile broadly and say, "Let all creation praise the beauty of the things I have made! Not only should all things encourage and praise each other, but let them also see and praise the sons and daughters who can praise My grace!" is it not the hope of humanity to have such a day that reveals God's authority and glory?  
However, when that hope is placed before the whole, glory has turned into lamentation, hope has turned into despair, and the heart of filial piety has turned into a heart of curse. Therefore, the question of who will resolve that realm of lamentation is a most serious issue.  
Since it is God's wish to meet such a day, the joy of welcoming sons and daughters who can fulfill such filial piety, and the glory of being able to call my beloved sons and daughters who can be the source of life for the universe while shedding tears of gratitude, is it not the heart of a parent who wishes to bestow that joy upon them? Is it not the greatest hope that humanity longs for to seek such a position? Exactly so.  
The central figures of the providential history who have walked a lonely and miserable path  
From that perspective, we humans have fallen. We have forsaken Heaven and created a realm of lamentation. Paul has already proclaimed this. He said that all creation laments. It has been said that all spirits in the spirit world, including the Holy Spirit, also lament. When we humans lament, we cannot deny that God, who looks upon this world, also laments. The descendants who have inherited such a history of lamentation have never once walked the path to resolve that lamentation. They have repeatedly experienced a history of failure.  
Due to the fall of Adam and Eve, in the history of Cain and Abel, God witnessed yet another secondary failure. Cain killed Abel, leading to a tragic scene. Although blood was not shed due to the fall, humanity has seen bloodshed as a result of the fall throughout history. Moreover, humans, who should reconcile with each other over the history of bloodshed, have failed to reconcile and have not united with Heaven. For this reason, God had to strike that humanity, centering on Noah, and thus became a God who had to wipe everything away until it was all gone.  
Even though He created humans with the utmost sincerity and made all things as objects of love and blessing for humanity, the fact that God had to take up a whip to judge them indicates that a history of lamentation filled with bloodshed has been inflicted upon them.  
To resolve such a history of lamentation, God chose Abraham and made him live a life of wandering. Thus, Abraham had to walk the miserable path of a traveler, leaving behind his beloved land and hometown.  
For this reason, the path that Abraham walked was a miserable one. He had to cross borders. He had to join the ranks of gypsies. He could not escape the status of a wanderer in a foreign land. Moreover, due to Pharaoh's cunning schemes, he was driven to the point of losing his wife and isolating his clan.  
Because the path of Heaven was a miserable one, those who followed Him could not escape misery. The path of the Israelite people was also miserable. The path of Moses was miserable. After 40 years in Pharaoh's palace, Moses was expelled and found himself in a fate where he could not reveal himself to the Israelite people, living as a shepherd in the Midian wilderness. He was trapped in a miserable living environment.  
Furthermore, we must understand that God chose numerous ancestors who came forward to fulfill His will, especially the miserable shepherd David, and placed him in a position to lead Israel. He was a lonely shepherd. He was not born into a position where he could be friends with anyone.  
However, in caring for the nation, he stood in a position of loneliness and admired Heaven from a solitary place. Deep in his heart, he was concerned about God's lamentation and prayed with a deep heart to alleviate God's concern for the Israelite people.  
When the giant Goliath of the Philistines boldly disregarded the Israelite people, and the Israelite army stood on the brink of annihilation, David appeared dressed as a shepherd with a sling and a stone. The one he took as his master was not a man. He did not receive the authority of a nation. He set Heaven as his true master. He believed in Heaven more than anyone among his ancestors. He knew that Heaven was alive. Even when faced with death, he believed that Heaven would protect him.  
Standing in such a position, David's path was lonely, yet he was not alone. It was miserable, yet he was not miserable. By doing so, he could resolve Heaven's lamentation and protect these people, thus finding a way to alleviate Heaven's sorrow. Because of this belief, Heaven was with David. That is why, no matter how formidable Goliath was, he could not help but fall before David like a mere piece of straw.  
We know that Heaven has hidden such miserable historical stories. In such miserable positions, God protected them, and He saw the revival of those who were oppressed.  
The path that Heaven walks is one that steps over the realm of lamentation and pioneers a day of victory.  
God blessed Jacob. The blessed Jacob went to Haran and walked a path of suffering for 21 years. He was deceived by Laban ten times and walked the path of persecution. He participated in a sorrowful position. He was trapped in a lonely place. From the perspective of his environment, he stood in a position where he faced lamentation and despair. However, if Jacob had become one who lamented in despair or one who blamed himself, he would not have been able to claim the national authority representing Israel.  
Even in the path of suffering that lasted for 20 years, Jacob believed until the end that Heaven's blessing would not change. He believed that no matter how much the environment changed, it would not change. No matter what wealth blocked his way, he pushed through. Laban was bound to raise other issues to block Jacob's path. However, in the end, the victory did not go to Laban but to Jacob.  
It was because, without bringing about such historical results, there could be no day of victory for God left in history. Therefore, the foundation upon which the lamenting Heaven could achieve victory is a history established when the lamenting multitude does not despair.  
Although Jacob was caught in the realm of lamentation of despair, he did not lament, nor did he despair; he stood confidently believing in the future blessing. Therefore, we must recognize that the first Israel was established.  
God is the same. No matter how deeply God is immersed in the realm of lamentation, He has not lost hope because of that lamentation. He has not lost the ideal of creation because of that lamentation. The stronger the lamentation, the more intense it becomes, the more He has made an inner resolution to fulfill the ideal of creation centered on heart and ideals.  
For this reason, the path that Heaven walks may be caught in the whirlpool of the realm of lamentation, but it does not merge with it; rather, it steps over that realm of lamentation and pioneers a day of victory.  
If that does not happen, there is no way for God to absolutely escape the realm of lamentation. Therefore, even in the extreme positions of despair and suffering, those who hold onto Heaven and believe, "You are a God who does not despair even in such a position, a God who does not lose hope, and a God who is stimulated in the place of lamentation," will surely be granted victory.  
Moses, who stood at the forefront of the nation with autonomous authority  
The history of Moses also reflects this. While living as a shepherd in the Midian wilderness after leaving the palace, what was the one heart he cherished? He did not despair because he had become that way while siding with the Israelite people. He did not think that his situation was due to the Israelite people. This is where Moses could receive God's trust. Although the fault lay with the Israelite people, he thought that he had become this way because of God, that his loneliness was felt to take responsibility for God's loneliness, and that his suffering was endured as a shield to defend against God's misery.  
With such a heart, while leading the flock of sheep for 40 years, why would there not be wolf attacks, and why would there not be threats from snakes? However, no matter how much danger increased and loneliness and lamentation swirled around, he thought that his situation was not due to the Israelite people but because of God. This great inner awakening led Moses to think, "I will be faithful until the day God's will is fulfilled."  
Thus, the Israelite people, who were to inherit God's will, faced him. He stood at the forefront of the nation with autonomous authority, saying, "I have come forth for the sake of Israel, ultimately for the sake of God's will." He was Moses, who had the inner and outer mental attitude to stand proudly before any number of nations.  
As ten years passed, twenty years went by, and thirty and forty years flowed, Moses reflected on his past life of luxury in Pharaoh's palace without purpose and thought, "I must not become one who admires Pharaoh's palace."  
The more the path of suffering that lay before him increased, the more he surely admired a palace that could command heaven and earth, the ideal of living in the Pharaoh's palace, the nation that God desired. On the day when the Israelite monarchy was liberated, he would have admired a global sovereign nation that could exalt that authority.  
Anyone who was subject to his ideology would have to follow Moses' thoughts and traditions, even those born as descendants of the twelve tribes of Israel, inheriting the profound heart from ancient times and possessing privileged authority. Wasn't it God who commanded Moses to be the representative of Israel? You must understand this.

He lived according to his father's will, so is he a person who acted freely or a person who acted in bondage? He acted in bondage. **The Path of Life**

<Words> Whether looking at our individual selves living on this earth, or looking at a nation, or looking at the entire world, we can see that neither the individual nor the nation nor the world exists because they want to exist. They did not form such a nation because they desired it.
They did not want it, but when they stand in the position that resulted from their ancestors, or from the history of humanity that did not want it, they naturally come to love that nation and think of that world.
When we look at our individual selves, we did not come into this world because we wanted to. Centered on our parents, if they are a people, or humanity, we exist on this earth, and it is inevitable that there must be a succeeding generation to carry on the lineage, because this is the path that heaven and humanity must take, and thus we were born as individuals following that path.
Before there is an individual, there are parents. Before parents, there are ancestors. If we pursue this upward, we eventually reach the founding ancestors of our Republic of Korea, passing through Dangun, and ultimately to Adam and Eve, the first ancestors of humanity.
When we look at Adam and Eve, they did not come into existence because they wanted to. There must be some cause that brought them into being, and it is to connect the purpose of that cause and the relationship with that cause that humans are born today. In this light, we cannot deny that we humans are ultimately beings of results.
It is an undeniable fact that I did not originate from myself. Whether viewed through a comprehensive historical perspective or through individual experiences, it is a fact that cannot be denied. I was born not for myself but according to some higher cause. Moreover, I was born not to go for myself but to follow some higher cause through a process to reach the purpose or result that cause seeks. Since that cause must progress and develop as desired, each of us, possessing the life of that process, must inevitably go through that process and reach the position of that purpose.
In such a context, I am connected to that. When viewed from my perspective, I represent us. You must always remember that an individual represents the whole.
The human desire is also connected to some cause.
From this perspective, each of us desires to be perfect without exception. No one wishes to be imperfect. When we look at our faces in the mirror, we see all our features and wish that our face looked like this or that, or that our eyes, nose, mouth, and entire being looked a certain way.
In addition to wishing for our external appearance, we also have our own desires regarding the internal state of our hearts. We wish to become a certain kind of person, to go to certain places our hearts desire, and to become a central being with certain values.
While that desire is centered on me, you must understand that it does not solely pertain to me. That desire must necessarily connect with a cause, and because that cause follows an unchanging path toward a clear purpose, we must always align ourselves with that path.
Where is the standard of having a straight and righteous heart?
You say that people should have a straight heart. You also say that they should have a righteous heart. However, we have yet to establish what that standard of straightness is. When we consider where the standard of righteousness lies, most people tend to define it based on the individual self.
Where should the standard of righteousness begin? It should begin from the cause. To draw a correct line from that cause, there must be a straight line leading to the purpose. A straight line is defined as a line connecting two points. Therefore, there must be a correct line that can lead to the result through the process of the cause. Only by drawing such a line can we establish what is straight and righteous.
People must become righteous and straight. What does it mean to be straight? It means to stand upright. We say a tree is straight, or a flagpole is straight. What does that mean? Straightness and righteousness refer to a point that is established in all directions around a 90-degree angle from the horizontal plane, connecting to a 360-degree shape.
When we connect straightness and righteousness from this perspective, it naturally forms a cross shape. Connecting straightness and righteousness can also form a square or a circle. When expressed in three dimensions, it becomes a sphere. Everything that extends from the center to the east, west, south, and north is the same everywhere, without gaps. It is perfect everywhere. This is what we pursue.
When viewed from the perspective of oneself, a person wishes for the boundary lines extending east and west to be the same. They wish for the boundary lines extending above and below to be the same. That is why everything resembles a circle. Everything moves according to a spherical shape. When considering this, no matter how large the world is, or how vast the directions of east, west, south, and north are, if I stand in the center, those boundary points are determined around me. No matter how high it may be, our human heart desires to establish such a relationship.
Everything moves according to a spherical shape.
Do you wish for the east or west to be confined and settled, so that the east remains only the east? No, that is not the case. When people are happy, they are bound to move. There is no one who remains still while being happy. When one dances or sings, their facial expressions already harmonize.
When a person smiles, it is not just the eyes or nose; the whole face smiles. When the face smiles, it is not just the face that smiles; the entire body harmonizes, interacts, and the shape of the whole being is manifested, which we always understand in our daily lives.
When a person is joyful, it is not just the heart that rejoices; the whole being rejoices. When one is sad, it is not just the heart that feels sorrow; the body also feels sorrow. When we consider this, we realize that our individual joy is not just an individual joy; that sorrow and joy are connected with the entire world.
In other words, if the cause and result are connected in an inseparable process, leading to the fulfillment of that purpose, then one appearance, one manifestation, one action in that process does not end with that process; it must influence the cause and affect the result. When someone finds something good, they do not simply say, "Ah, this is good!" and leave it at that. When we look at the human heart, we wish to leave something good for eternity.
Because today was good, we hope that tomorrow will be the same, and thus we have a desire for the entire year, ten years, and our whole lives to be good. We can see that this goodness does not wish to remain within the limits of a temporary condition.
Our human lives do not demand a moment of joy that is limited by any environment, any framework, or any boundary. Rather, we wish to connect with joy that can extend beyond that position, reaching out to the whole front in all directions.
Only a public life can remain forever with history.
Therefore, joy should not remain as just today's joy. That joy must be eternally connected. However, sorrow should not be eternally connected. Sorrow must be resolved quickly.
Because we must leave joy and resolve sorrow, when we consider the unforgettable things that remain in our lives, we can identify three things: the times we were the happiest, the times we were the saddest, and the times we faced the greatest difficulties.
When we consider the hardships people have faced, there are two types of difficulties. One is the difficulty faced for oneself, and the other is the difficulty faced for the whole, such as the nation. Difficulties faced for oneself end with the individual. We know well that such difficulties cannot establish connections with others.
However, if one has faced difficulties for the whole beyond the individual, we know that it establishes a relationship with the entirety. Ultimately, patriotism...
through the path of life, it is important to understand that those who have taken on the responsibility to solve the difficulties of the whole, rather than just following their personal struggles, are true patriots. The hardships faced in such positions represent the struggles of the whole, and we know well that they create connections with the entirety.

Among such patriots, those who have suffered the most become even greater patriots. A dutiful child, if they can dedicate themselves to their parents in difficult situations, reveals a higher value of filial piety, especially when the situation is dire. From this perspective, we must recognize that all suffering can be categorized into two types: personal suffering, which disappears with the individual, and suffering endured for the whole, which does not vanish until the entirety itself is gone.

Thus, whether it is a nation striving to leave a tradition or humanity aiming to establish a legacy in the face of world history, we cannot deny that historical standards are established through enduring public hardships. In other words, those who sacrifice their lives for the sake of all humanity, transcending their individual selves, create a foundational point that humanity cannot overlook. Such individuals naturally become subjects of remembrance in historical times, leaving a path for future generations to follow.

When we consider our lives, what remains are joyful experiences, sorrowful moments, and hardships. If these are the elements that persist in our lives, then extending such experiences collectively with all humanity becomes our shared history. Therefore, what remains in human history is akin to what remains in our individual lives. Consequently, the events that endure the longest in the historical process are those that were the most difficult.

When we look at ourselves as individuals, what remains next? It is the saddest moments. Just as the most profoundly sorrowful events in our lives are unforgettable, the saddest occurrences in historical times also endure. What remains is not personal sorrow but public sorrow. Those who have endured for such causes remain in history alongside it.

Therefore, while personal sorrow may linger in an individual's life, it ultimately ends with that life. However, those who carry public sorrow continue to exist alongside world history, even after their death. This is an unavoidable truth. The more individuals who have fought to alleviate the sorrow of the world for the sake of humanity, forgetting themselves even in their demise, the more they become representatives of the sorrows of historical times. We must recognize that figures like Jesus are indeed such representatives.

Next, what remains is joy. The joys experienced in your life endure. Most people measure their lives by their personal joys or aim for them, but our human history is different. Joy centered around personal experiences does not endure; it ends with the individual. When a personal life concludes, that joy flows away. However, if one seeks a position from which they can rejoice on behalf of all humanity, and if they establish a form of joyful life to leave behind, the more public that life is, the more it remains in human history.

Thus, figures like Jesus, who suffered more than anyone else and lived a sorrowful life, wished for joy to be shared with humanity. They hoped that joy would extend from before history to after it, and they pursued that joy. They dedicated their lives to it and made every sacrifice for it. As the saying goes, "Where there is sincerity, there is divine favor," Jesus invested his intellect for that one purpose, ensuring that the world of that purpose would not vanish but would develop into a historical era that could meet the dawn of a distant future. Because they pursued such a path with humanity, it is an undeniable fact that they formed a global Christian cultural sphere that transcended from one clan to one nation.

This did not happen because the deceased Jesus had power, nor did he manage that path. It can be concluded that it is inevitable as long as there is a divine principle and God exists. <Prayer> Father, we have not had a single day of joy inherited from You. We did not know how happy You are, nor did we know how precious Your love is. We also did not know the right path You must take.
Now, standing at this final destination at the end of the era, we must be able to draw the ideal world of your original creative nature that can align with the circumstances of the Father, who must immediately make a new start. 

In doing so, the serious life-and-death issue of overcoming the world stands in our way. The sad problem of the world's misfortune lies before us. Our sorrow no longer ends with our own sorrow. The cries of suffering from the Republic of Korea resonate throughout the world. Now, the world is paying attention to the path of suffering that the Republic of Korea must take.

When we look at this process, the groups for unification today have been carrying the tremendous task of returning to the nation since the day the Unification Church began, persistently enduring opposition, and have not been driven out before this nation, but have stuck like a leech, connecting to the world stage and developing.

Now, as we realize that the fortune of the Unification Church can rapidly develop into an environment larger than that of the Republic of Korea, we feel the responsibility from within and without to prepare for the path of suffering that the Republic of Korea must defend in the future.

Father, have mercy on your children here in the homeland! Now we understand that wherever we go, we must become one inside and out. We also know that you have gone seven years ahead. From now until 1978, there is a historic responsibility to determine the fate of the world, and we have understood that the period of your providence for restoration is set until then, so we intend to go until that time. Furthermore, we must go until 1981, when the third seven-year course ends.

In the path that this nation and this people must take in the future, we know that it is a time to discern whether we will rise to the top of the world by 1981 or not. Father, if that connection is made, by 1984, we must establish a decisive fate in the historical process, or we will not feel the worth of our lives. This is the inevitable and decisive path we must take.

Therefore, even if the wind blows, we must understand that it is a wind that blows for fear we might doze off. Or if a storm rages, we must realize that it is a warning to come out of the house because staying inside will lead to ruin. Everything that comes at us is understood as the final connection of encouragement from the Father, and I know that we must become a group that can absorb this.

Every time I bow my head before the Father, who has led me along a path that no one knows until now, I am filled with awe. If I had not met you, I would not have worked for decades in the modern history of Korea.

Because of your historical connection that came to this people, and because you are a Father who has compassion for this people that has gone through painful circumstances, this people has overcome a path of suffering unknown to anyone, having gone through a history of five thousand years in Asia, and they are a nation that wishes to boast of the appearance of a prosperous country, possessing a patriotism that lifts high in the heavens, yet they are a people who do not know how to invade another country centered around a single sovereignty. Therefore, you cannot help but love the Korean people more than any other nation in the historical era. Because they are a people who can connect with your circumstances, I understand that this nation and this people are those you have had compassion for over a long history.

In the aftermath of the suffering endured from Japan at the end of the colonial period, you established a historical connection before this people, knowing that many have taken on the mission of martyrdom in the world history and walk the path of death with you. Thus, if this people had followed your will today and walked hand in hand with the Unification Church, this nation would have become a restored heaven.

If the Unification Church had grown to one hundred million, the Republic of Korea would have become heaven. If the world had formed a new cultural sphere centered around the Unification Church, this world would have moved under our command.

Father! This nation has been one that could not welcome the path you have sought for decades. Because I have taken on the responsibility of representing that failure to welcome, I have come out hoping that the nation would be right, fearing that the nation might perish, and I have volunteered to fall so that the nation would not fall. Thus, now we know that we must go to the final battlefield that awaits us, bearing the body that has been wounded and broken.

Overcoming the path of tears while enduring the trials of the nation and the sufferings of the church and society… Our lives, filled with sorrows that cannot be compared to anyone else, and our sad lives, have been lonely, but I know you have been lonelier and that you have been sadder. Therefore, we must be able to imagine the sorrow of the Father who endures the path of loneliness for eternity from that lonely position.

You, Father, know our hearts that tried to comfort you even in loneliness. We feel that you are a pitiful Father who cannot abandon the Unification Church, and so we have comforted you with tears even on the right path, and even as we move on the path of being pursued, we have been following this historical path of your sorrowful exile, trying to comfort your historical heart. Knowing the path that the sons and daughters who must leave a legacy must take, we wished for ruin, but even in the place of ruin, we did not perish. If there was a way to die for the world, we wished to die ourselves, but because you have a purpose to leave us and a mission to fulfill this purpose, you have spared us from death. I have understood that to pass that place, you must endure trials greater than death.

Every time events that could conflict in a million ways come crashing down, we have understood the feelings of Elijah, who said, "Am I the only one left?" When we are left in a lonely position that no one can fulfill, we think of the times you came to comfort us, knowing that you were greatly concerned that your poor sons and daughters might betray you. Every time I think of that, I resolve that even if I die a million times, I will not pray for my comfort and salvation on the path of death. This is the wish of this child who has been leading the Unification Church, and you know that.

Father! Since the day I learned of your sorrow in losing both the nation and the church and seeking the prison as a path with no way to go, I have not yet fulfilled my determination to resolve this grievance, so I must hasten the time day and night, knowing that it is my responsibility as this child leading the Unification Church.

Knowing that the path we have come has been rough, the path ahead will be even rougher, we must endure and overcome the path of coming and going. We know that if we despair today, we cannot resolve tomorrow's sorrow, so we must greet today's despair with joy. This is the path that those who are unfaithful to you must take. However, beyond the history of the misfortune of restoration that you could not welcome, I am a poor child who has never called you from a position of freedom, peace, and happiness, where you can embrace and love me with a smile, saying, "My beloved son."

If I could call you Father and die in such a position, that would be your wish, and what greater glory could there be? Knowing that this is the wish of all people today, I understand that I must not die or fall until that position is reached.

Having come this far through half a century of life, I know that you will walk with me again to the world stage we must go to. If there is another path of tears, you must shed tears, and if there is a lonely circumstance, you must endure loneliness. When I think that you must always be there to guide the path of the future, which cannot avoid the path of being an unfilial child, I hope that even if I must bear the greatest cross of preparation, I can find a way to serve the unchanging heaven. Please remember this nation along with your granted will!

Every path I take is for loving the nation and opening the future path of the nation, and I must determine the place that will decide life and death until the last moment from a pitiful position, and I know that it is the path I must take for these people. Therefore, I cannot forget this land anywhere I go, and I cannot help but think of this place. Now, once I go, the day we part awaits us. A decisive path of relentless advance lies behind us, so for that path, I must settle the past sins and face the destiny path ahead, pledging the final victory and preparing for the appearance of heaven's peace and rest.

Father, today, tomorrow, the day after tomorrow, and until the 15th, please encourage the members across the nation. We must become one. Whether young or old, we must unite. Regardless of gender or age, we must become one. I think of the command of the Father to place the university students of the Principle Research Association on the front lines and to drive them out again. Until now, they have acted on their own, but from now on, I hope that they can become a group of children who absolutely comply with the national and global fortune before us, following the laws of righteousness and overcoming the final peak.

As we look toward the remaining restored heaven, please allow us to become a group that marches forth with the spirit of the strong before the last remaining front line, as heavenly soldiers. Thus, as a group that carries the hope of tomorrow before the world of meaningful purpose entrusted to us, please guide us to become a group that is trustworthy in your eyes and worthy of your praise, and I earnestly ask you to entrust us with responsibilities, all in the name of True Parents. Amen.
